	<script type="text/javascript">
    function randomDisplay(className) {
   // Get all the features
   var features = $(className);

   // Pick a random feature
   var num = Math.floor( Math.random() * features.length );
   
   // Display the randomly selected feature and hide all the other ones
   $(className).hide().eq(num).show();
   
   // Remove all the hidden features
   $(className).filter(function() {
       return $(this).css('display') == 'none';
   }).remove();
}
    randomDisplay(".jsQuote");
</script>

<section class="innerSection borderTop">
	<div class="wrap">
	    <div class="articleContent">
	   	    
	    	       
	        	            <p>CMU-Africa&#8217;s vision is to educate and empower the next generation of African leaders and innovators by delivering a world-class educational experience. Our mission is to produce creative and technically strong engineers, who have been trained in the African context and prepared to make a transformative impact in their communities and the world.</p>
<p>In 2011, upon the invitation of the Government of Rwanda (GoR), Carnegie Mellon and the GoR signed an agreement to establish a new CMU location in Kigali, Rwanda. This ambitious and innovative partnership was designed to respond to the critical shortage of high-quality engineering talent required to harness Africa&#8217;s tremendous potential as home to the fastest-growing workforce in the world.</p>
<p>CMU-Africa, located in <a href="living-in-rwanda/kigali-innovation-city.html">Kigali Innovation City</a>, is a regional ICT center of excellence educating a diverse composition of future leaders from all over Africa, who will use their hands-on skills and knowledge to advance technology innovation and grow businesses.</p>
<p>Carnegie Mellon University&#8217;s presence in Rwanda continues to provide a platform to engage in Africa&#8217;s most significant opportunities and challenges through world-class education and contextually relevant research.</p>

        		        		            		<div class="contactShout">

 <section class="innerSection borderTop">  
    <div class="wrap">
		<h2 class="heading3">About the College of Engineering at Carnegie Mellon University</h2>
	
		
	                               
              	     <div class="articleContent">
    	             <div class="figureMedium alignRight">
            	            	<figure>	
            	    <img alt="CMU campus" src="../_files/images/about/pittsburgh-campus.jpg"/>	
            		<figcaption>
            			<p class="figSource"><strong>Source: </strong> Carnegie Mellon University</p>
            			            			    <p class="figCaption">Carnegie Mellon University is a private research university based in Pittsburgh, Pennsylvania.</p>
            			            		</figcaption>	
            	</figure>
            </div>
         <p>The world-class <a href="https://engineering.cmu.edu/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">College of Engineering</a> is recognized for excellence, innovation, and the societal relevance of its pursuits. We produce creative and technically strong engineers, and smart solutions to global challenges. We do this with an unprecedented drive to integrate engineering, sciences, arts, business and other disciplines to produce transformative results.</p>
<p>With cutting-edge information security, innovative start-ups, big data, hands-on learning, and creative mobile applications, CMU doesn't imagine the future&#8211;CMU creates it.</p>
<p>Learn more about <a href="https://www.cmu.edu/about/history.html">the history of Carnegie Mellon University</a> and <a href="https://engineering.cmu.edu/about-us/history.html">the College of Engineering</a>.</p>
<p>&#160;</p>
      </div>
     </div>
 </section>

	<script type="text/javascript">
    function randomDisplay(className) {
   // Get all the features
   var features = $(className);

   // Pick a random feature
   var num = Math.floor( Math.random() * features.length );
   
   // Display the randomly selected feature and hide all the other ones
   $(className).hide().eq(num).show();
   
   // Remove all the hidden features
   $(className).filter(function() {
       return $(this).css('display') == 'none';
   }).remove();
}
    randomDisplay(".jsQuote");
</script>

    function randomDisplay(className) {
   // Get all the features
   var features = $(className);

   // Pick a random feature
   var num = Math.floor( Math.random() * features.length );
   
   // Display the randomly selected feature and hide all the other ones
   $(className).hide().eq(num).show();
   
   // Remove all the hidden features
   $(className).filter(function() {
       return $(this).css('display') == 'none';
   }).remove();
}
    randomDisplay(".jsQuote");

                	    <h1 class="medHeadline">Research</h1>

<section class="innerSection borderTop">
	<div class="wrap">
	    <div class="articleContent">
	   	    
	    	       
	        	            CMU-Africa is home to world-class experts and thought leaders who are tackling challenges across the continent and around the globe. CMU-Africa faculty, students, and alumni are actively engaged in projects that respond to the challenges and opportunities of the digital transformation of Africa.
                    	       
	        			    	
	 	    <h2>Research thrusts</h2>
<p>&#160;</p>
	 	 <div class="iconThrusts">
                                  <div>
              	<p>
              	    		                <img alt="Computer icon" class="largeIcon" height="300" src="../_files/icons/laptop-icon.png" width="300"/>
		            		        </p>
		                    <p><strong>Cybersecurity:</strong> CMU-Africa is developing context-aware security and privacy solutions for a more resilient African cyberspace.
                                                                                                            
                                           <a href="cybersecurity/index.html" rel="noopener">Learn more</a>
                                                   </p>
                       </div>
                                 <div>
              	<p>
              	    		                <img alt="Battery icon" class="largeIcon" height="300" src="../_files/icons/battery-icon.png" width="300"/>
		            		        </p>
		                    <p><strong>Energy and mobility:</strong> The future of energy and mobility can learn from current African examples. Our study of the context and drivers helps us identify new challenges and opportunities.
                                                                                                
                                           <a href="energy.html" rel="noopener">Learn more</a>
                                                   </p>
                       </div>
                                 <div>
              	<p>
              	    		                <img alt="Wifi icon" class="largeIcon" height="300" src="../_files/icons/informationcomm-icon.png" width="300"/>
		            		        </p>
		                    <p><strong>Information and communications technology:</strong> CMU-Africa is a regional ICT center of excellence educating future leaders from all over Africa, who will use their hands-on skills and knowledge to advance technology innovation and grow businesses.
                                                                                                
                                           <a href="ict.html" rel="noopener">Learn more</a>
                                                   </p>
                       </div>
                                 <div>
              	<p>
              	    		                <img alt="robot arm" class="largeIcon" height="300" src="../_files/icons/ai-robots-icon.png" width="300"/>
		            		        </p>
		                    <p><strong>AI and robotics:</strong> Faculty and students are working to obtain a deeper understanding of complex systems and leverage sustainable AI-based solutions, such as robotics, for assisting people and improving productivity.
                                                                                                
                                           <a href="artificial-intelligence.html" rel="noopener">Learn more</a>
                                                   </p>
                       </div>
            </div>
     				    
			        	       
	        	            <h2>Watch research videos from CMU-Africa</h2>
                    	       
	                        <div class="videoContain baseVideo">
					<div class="videoEmbed fitvid">
					    					        <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="315" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/PLAVlq43fXEH23pQ7UBo3najt0EHsNeIvW?list=PLAVlq43fXEH23pQ7UBo3najt0EHsNeIvW" width="560"></iframe>
					    					</div><!-- videoEmbed -->
				</div><!-- videoContain -->	
			         	       
	        	            <h2>The Sustainable Development Goals</h2>
<p>Carnegie Mellon University is committed to supporting the Sustainable Development Goals (SDGs) through <a href="https://www.cmu.edu/leadership/the-provost/provost-priorities/sustainability-initiative/index.html">the Sustainability Initiative at CMU</a>. The <a href="https://sdgs.un.org/goals" rel="noopener" target="_blank">SDGs</a>, also known as the Global Goals, are 17 global objectives to create a more equitable and viable planet by 2030. These goals came together following input from millions of people around the world, with younger generations especially engaged. They were adopted by the global community at the United Nations in 2015.</p>
                    	       
	                        <div class="videoContain baseVideo">
					<div class="videoEmbed fitvid">
					    						    <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="315" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/94pwSsaZmX4" width="560"></iframe>
											</div><!-- videoEmbed -->
				</div><!-- videoContain -->	
			         	       
	        	            <p>At CMU-Africa, the SDGs set out clear objectives for researchers working in the African context. They are focused on positive societal outcomes that apply to Africa and the global community. The SDGs set a mindset for researchers to think beyond specific technical questions and consider the potential of their work in society.</p>
<p>With the common language of the SDGs, researchers can speak with each other and identify collaborators across geographic and disciplinary divides. In these ways, the SDG framework is the key to unlocking the potential of the diverse research of CMU-Africa faculty.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=FCx736AKYdY&amp;list=PLAVlq43fXEH3PWisdHteIYbxKURkF5cm9"><strong>Learn more about what the SDGs mean to the CMU-Africa community.</strong></a></p>
                    	       
	        	            <h2>Kigali Collaborative Research Centre (KCRC)</h2>
<p><a href="https://www.kcrc.rw/">KCRC</a><a href="https://www.kcrc.rw/?page_id=86"></a> and CMU-Africa have a shared mission to enable collaborative research and innovations in Africa. The center, located in <a href="../about/living-in-rwanda/kigali-innovation-city.html">Kigali Innovation City</a>, aims to be a leading research organization in Africa dedicated to establishing and facilitating high standards and diverse research and innovations.</p>
<p>For more information, contact <a href="../about/contact/directory/bios/brown-tim.html">Timothy Brown</a>,&#160;director of KCRC</p>
                          </div> <!--article Content-->
	</div><!-- wrap -->
</section><!-- fullContain -->

	<script type="text/javascript">
    function randomDisplay(className) {
   // Get all the features
   var features = $(className);

   // Pick a random feature
   var num = Math.floor( Math.random() * features.length );
   
   // Display the randomly selected feature and hide all the other ones
   $(className).hide().eq(num).show();
   
   // Remove all the hidden features
   $(className).filter(function() {
       return $(this).css('display') == 'none';
   }).remove();
}
    randomDisplay(".jsQuote");
</script>

   <div class="mediaBlock">
                                            <a href="https://spaceinafrica.com/2024/10/03/star-visions-spaceborne-ai-algorithm-rideshare-programme-enters-development-phase/" target="_blank">
                            	     <p class="mdb-cat">Space in Africa</p>
                	        <h3 class="mdb-headline">CMU-Africa students develop spaceborne AI algorithm </h3>
            		</a>
    	    	<p class="mdb-content">CMU-Africa students participated in a collaborative project, STAR.VISION, as reported by Space in Africa. Under the mentorship of Rwanda Space Agency (RSA) engineers, students developed algorithms for the project’s inaugural AI Algorithm Rideshare Programme 1.0. 
</p>
    </div>
   
        				                 		             		                                    				    
   <div class="mediaBlock">
                                            <a href="https://www.biometricupdate.com/202409/biometric-authentication-invaluable-set-to-further-enhance-security-in-africa" target="_blank">
                            	     <p class="mdb-cat">Biometric Update</p>
                	        <h3 class="mdb-headline">Upanzi Network hosts hackathon webinar</h3>
            		</a>
    	    	<p class="mdb-content">Upanzi Network's recent webinar for the Eastern Africa Digital ID Hackathon was reported on by Biometric Update. Throughout this webinar, experts discussed the importance of biometric authentication and the Modular Open Source Identity Platform (MOSIP).
</p>
    </div>
   
        				                 		             		                                    				    
   <div class="mediaBlock">
                                            <a href="https://medium.com/authority-magazine/defeating-deepfakes-conrad-tucker-of-carnegie-mellon-university-how-we-can-identify-convincingly-a7542cd17a5f" target="_blank">
                            	     <p class="mdb-cat">Medium</p>
                	        <h3 class="mdb-headline">Tucker discusses deepfakes</h3>
            		</a>
    	    	<p class="mdb-content">CMU-Africa Director Conrad Tucker spoke with Medium about his work and strategies for the public to protect themselves against deepfakes and disinformation. “Policies need to be established to protect users so that they can be confident that the content they are consuming can be trusted,” Tucker says. 
</p>
    </div>

	<script type="text/javascript">
    function randomDisplay(className) {
   // Get all the features
   var features = $(className);

   // Pick a random feature
   var num = Math.floor( Math.random() * features.length );
   
   // Display the randomly selected feature and hide all the other ones
   $(className).hide().eq(num).show();
   
   // Remove all the hidden features
   $(className).filter(function() {
       return $(this).css('display') == 'none';
   }).remove();
}
    randomDisplay(".jsQuote");
</script>

    <script src="https://engineering.cmu.edu/departments/_files/js/script-min.js"></script>
	<script type="text/javascript">
    function randomDisplay(className) {
   // Get all the features
   var features = $(className);

   // Pick a random feature
   var num = Math.floor( Math.random() * features.length );
   
   // Display the randomly selected feature and hide all the other ones
   $(className).hide().eq(num).show();
   
   // Remove all the hidden features
   $(className).filter(function() {
       return $(this).css('display') == 'none';
   }).remove();
}
    randomDisplay(".jsQuote");
</script>
